  cache-error-config threshold-num 3000 reboot enable

  url-db-query server1 enable

exit
no sms disable
ha link interface aggregate4
ha link ip 10.255.255.1 255.255.255.252
ha group 0
  arp 30
  monitor track "HA"
exit
ha cluster 1

End
DC1B1FW-LMWL-SS6~(M)#
